 Schizophrenia seems like a complicated word to read
 jise bolne main jubaan jaraa si ladkadaati he
 In Hindi it can be called schizophrenia
 medical kii bhashaa main agar ise samajhane kii koshish karen to yah ek maansik beemaari he
 The person suffering from this disease forgets to understand real and imaginary things
 kai baar vah yun hi khoyaa-khoyaa rahata he
 Under certain social circumstances, she is unable to decide what to react to
 aam manyata ke vipareet yah spolit persenality nahin he
 
 
 There is a common belief that Schizophrenia is Split personality or Multiple personality but it is not
 is beemaari se peedit log hinsak nahin hote or samaaj ke liye kisi tarah kaa khatra nahin hai
 The disease is not caused by childbirth, poor parenting or lack of willpower
 aakhir kya he Schizophrenia kii vajah?is beemaari ke kaaran abhi tak spasht nahin ho sake hai
 However, it is also attributed to genetics, brain chemistry, viral infections, carelessness during seasonal changes and digestive system disturbances
 kya hai is beemaari ke sanket?is beemaari main alag-alag shaks ke sanket bhi alag-alag hote hai
 In this, the system gradually appears within the people in months or years
 yah beemaari kuch aisi he ki aati-jaati rahati he
 To see and hear something that is not really there
 aapako aisa lagata ho jaise log aapako chhip kar dekh rahe hai
 Having a peculiar complexity in terms of writing and speaking
 sharir ko besange tareeke se rakhana
 Reacting differently on every important occasion
 padhai-likhaai se ekadam se anmana ho janaa
 Personality changes
 kinhin saamaajik jalson se cat kar rahanaa
 Being cut off from your near and dear ones
 sone yaa phir dhyaan kendrit karne main dikkatein aana
 Unnecessary attachment to mysterious things or religion
 aaj puri duniya kii jansankhya ke ek fisad log Schizophrenia se peedit hai

 aisa bhi nahin he ki yah kisi varg vishesh ke logon ke bich hi vyaapt he

 yah beemaari mahilaon kii tulana purushon main adhik dekhi jaati he

 is baar bhi vah sabarkantha seat se maidan main utar sakate hai

 Shankar Singh Vaghela started his political journey from the Emergency period
 gandhi nagar ke vaasan main rajput parivaar main janme waghela shuruyaat main rashtriya swayan sevak sangh ke sakriy sadsy the
 He also went to jail during the Emergency

 Vaghela was the vice president of the Janata Party in Gujarat and from 1980 to 1991 he was the general secretary and president of the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) in Gujarat
 vah 1984 se 1989 tak rajya sabha ke sadsy bhi rahe
 Vaghela won from Gandhinagar Lok Sabha seat in 1989 and Godhra Lok Sabha seat in 1991
 1995 main gujarat main jab bijepi ne 182 main se 121 siton par jeet darj kii, to vidhayakon waghela ko apana netaa chunaa tha, lekin sheersh netritv ne keshubhai patel ko siem kii kursi de di
 In September 1995, Vaghela revolted against the BJP leadership with the support of 47 mlas
 baad main samjhaute ke taur par waghela ke vafaadaar suresh mehta ko siem banaaya gaya, 1996 kaa loksabhaa chunaav waghela godhra seat se haar gaye or jald hi unhone apane samarthakon ke saath bhartiya janata party chhod di, jisase suresh mehta kii sarkaar gir gai
 After this Vaghela formed his own party under the name Rashtriya Janata Party and became the Chief Minister in October 1996 with the support of the Congress Party
 unhone 1997 kii shuruyaat main radhanpur seat se gujarat vidhansabha ke liye upachunaav jeeta, lekin oktober 1997 main gujarat main chal rahi raajnneetik uthal-puthal ke bich unhen mukhyamantri pad se istipha dena padaa or unke saathi baagi purv bijepi vidhayak dilip paarikh siem ban gaye

 upie sarkaar main unhen kendriya mantri banaaya gaya tha

 2012 ke gujarat vidhansabha main vah kapadvanj seat se chunaav lade or jite
